########## LIMITED REARMAMENT TREE ##########
	
	focus = {
		id = limited_rearmament_focus
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_build_tank
		x = 3
		y = 0
		cost = 40
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY }
		
		available_if_capitulated = yes
		
		complete_tooltip = {
		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			every_owned_state = { 
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = industrial_complex
						size > 1
						include_locked = yes
					}
					is_core_of = ROOT
					NOT = { has_state_category = tiny_island }
					NOT = { has_state_category = small_island }
				}
				random_select_amount = 5
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

					}

				custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_if_focus_raf_36
				effect_tooltip = {
					air_experience = 25
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						limit = {
							is_in_home_area = yes
							free_building_slots = {
								building = arms_factory
								size > 1
								include_locked = yes
							}
							NOT = { has_state_category = tiny_island }
							NOT = { has_state_category = small_island }
						}
						add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
						add_building_construction = {
							type = arms_factory
							level = 2
							instant_build = yes
						}
						set_state_flag = air_rearmament_focus_mil
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = ENG_focus_raf_1936
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = Line_break_keep_formating
				custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_branch_focused
				air_experience = 25
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						is_in_home_area = yes
						free_building_slots = {
							building = arms_factory
							size > 1
							include_locked = yes
						}
						NOT = { has_state_category = tiny_island }
						NOT = { has_state_category = small_island }
					}

	focus = {
		id = naval_rearmament_focus
		icon = GFX_goal_eng_battleship
		prerequisite = { focus = ENG_focus_army_1936 focus = ENG_focus_navy_1936 focus = ENG_focus_raf_1936 }
		relative_position_id = ENG_focus_navy_1936 
		x = 4
		y = 1
		cost = 40
		search_filters = {FOCUS_FILTER_NAVY}
		
		available = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_ai = no
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
					}
				}
				OR = {
					threat > 0.03
					date > 1937.1.1
				}
			}
			else = {
				OR = {
					threat > 0.03
					date > 1936.6.1
				}
			}
		}
		continue_if_invalid = yes
		available_if_capitulated = yes
		
		complete_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = ENG_focus_navy_1936
				}
				navy_experience = 50
			}
			else = {
				navy_experience = 25
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { has_state_flag = ENG_naval_rearmament_focus_1dockyard }
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { has_state_flag = ENG_naval_rearmament_focus_1capitalshipyard }
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = shipyard_capital_building
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		
		completion_reward = {
			navy_experience = 25
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				prioritize = { 133 }
				limit = {
					dockyard > 0
					is_core_of = ENG
					is_fully_controlled_by = ENG
					is_coastal = yes
					NOT = { has_state_category = tiny_island }
					NOT = { has_state_category = small_island }
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = shipyard_capital_building
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
				set_state_flag = ENG_naval_rearmament_focus_1capitalshipyard
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					is_coastal = yes
					free_building_slots = {
						building = dockyard
						size > 0
						include_locked = yes
					}
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
				set_state_flag = ENG_naval_rearmament_focus_1dockyard
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = ENG_focus_navy_1936
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = Line_break_keep_formating
				custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_if_focus_navy_36
				effect_tooltip = {
					navy_experience = 25
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						limit = {
							is_in_home_area = yes
							is_coastal = yes
							free_building_slots = {
								building = dockyard
								size > 0
								include_locked = yes
							}
						}
						add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
						add_building_construction = {
							type = dockyard
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
						set_state_flag = ENG_naval_rearmament_focus_1dockyard
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = ENG_focus_navy_1936
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = Line_break_keep_formating
				custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_branch_focused
				navy_experience = 25
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						is_in_home_area = yes
						is_coastal = yes

						}
					}

						level = 1

					}

				}

				}

					type = shipyard_capital_building

					instant_build = yes
				}
				set_state_flag = ENG_navy_mobilization_1capitalshipyard
			}

				prioritize = { 132 }
				limit = {
					dockyard > 0
					is_core_of = ENG
					is_fully_controlled_by = ENG

					NOT = { has_state_category = small_island }

########## Colonial / Commonwealth Ties Tree ##########
	
	focus = {
		id = uk_colonial_focus
		icon = GFX_goal_hat
		#prerequisite = { focus = uk_empire_focus }
		relative_position_id = uk_empire_focus
		x = -2
		y = 6
		cost = 20
		search_filters = {FOCUS_FILTER_RESEARCH}
		
		available_if_capitulated = yes
		
		completion_reward = {
			add_ideas = { ENG_colonial_elite }
			
			# needed for ai_strategy_plan
			hidden_effect = {
				set_temp_variable = { eng_global_or_home_def = 0 }
				randomize_temp_variable = {
					var = eng_global_or_home_def
					distribution = uniform
					min = 0
					max = 10
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							eng_global_or_home_def > 5
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = eng_support_home_def
				}
				else = {
